Current Commentary

Commemoration of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Birthday 52

—

Today is the commemoration of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's birthday. Dr. Sun Yat-sen was the creator of the Chinese Revolutionary Party and the creator of the Republic of China. Dr. Sun Yat-sen had a consistent and broad revolutionary doctrine, an indomitable and persistent revolutionary spirit, and a selfless and great personality. Dr. Sun Yat-sen was able to accept valuable lessons from history and constantly enrich the content of his revolutionary doctrine and revolutionary strategy according to the needs of objective facts. The National Revolution advocated by Dr. Sun Yat-sen for forty years is still the theme of the Chinese revolutionary problem. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's revolutionary doctrine and teachings are still deeply imprinted in the minds of the Chinese people. We only see Dr. Sun Yat-sen's piercing eyes and great and lofty personality. Dr. Sun's birth was the appearance of the savior of the Chinese nation. Now, although this bright savior has unfortunately fallen, the sparks burst out by the savior remain in the world like torches.

Today, as we commemorate Dr. Sun Yat-sen's birthday, it is a time when foreign troubles are deepening and the Chinese nation has reached a critical juncture of life and death. Therefore, in response to the current crisis, all Chinese who admire Dr. Sun Yat-sen should accept Dr. Sun Yat-sen's revolutionary doctrine and revolutionary spirit to continue to struggle and implement his valuable teachings to resolve the current national crisis and save the Chinese nation from subjugation.

What are the valuable teachings that Dr. Sun Yat-sen showed us?

First, Dr. Sun Yat-sen once said, "The Three Principles of the People are the doctrine of saving the country... Why do we say that the Three Principles of the People are the doctrine of saving the country? Because the Three Principles of the People are to promote China's equal international status, equal political status, and equal economic status, so that China can permanently survive in the world. Therefore, we say that the Three Principles of the People are the doctrine of saving the country." (The First Lecture on the Three Principles of the People and Nationalism) Now is the time to save the country and survive. The Three Principles of the People are by no means empty ideals, but the broad road that the Chinese revolution should take. Therefore, to realize the Three Principles of the People, the first step is to "save the country," that is, to save the country and survive. As the saying goes, "If the skin is gone, what will the hair cling to?" Today, as we commemorate Dr. Sun Yat-sen's birthday, our only task is to resist foreign aggression and defend the integrity of our territory.

Second, Dr. Sun Yat-sen told us in his will, "I have devoted myself to the national revolution for forty years. With forty years of experience, I know deeply that to achieve this goal, we must awaken the people... and fight together." In his repeated lectures, he repeatedly clarified the importance of "sovereignty in the people." In the declaration of going north, he further said, "From today onwards, we should inaugurate a new era of national revolution, so that the phenomenon of military force combining with imperialism will never appear in the country, and what will replace it will be the phenomenon of the first step of combining military force with the people, and the second step of making military force the military force of the people." At the same time, "Regarding the current situation, we advocate convening a national conference to seek China's unification and construction." Now is the time to gather the strength, wisdom, financial resources, and material resources of the whole country to save China from destruction. Therefore, as we read Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will, we sincerely hope that the government will lead the people, and the people will pledge to be the government's support, to rescue the dying China. To achieve this step, we naturally cannot lack the spirit of the Principle of People's Livelihood advocated by Dr. Sun Yat-sen, because only in this way can we make the "lower sentiments" "reach the top" and "unite the whole country with sincerity" to "go to the national crisis together."

Third, Dr. Sun Yat-sen repeatedly said when he was dying, "Peaceful struggle to save China." Dr. Sun Yat-sen was a pacifist, and his ultimate ideal was world communism. Dr. Sun Yat-sen also said in his will, "Unite with the nations of the world that treat me equally and fight together." Now the whole world is in the midst of a melee between the peace camp and the aggression camp. In order to protect the peace of East Asia and resist the enemy's aggression, between "enemy or friend," we should always uphold Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings to seek friends of the Chinese nation.

The above three points are all what the far-sighted Dr. Sun Yat-sen taught us long ago. When we commemorate Dr. Sun Yat-sen's birthday, we can only implement his teachings to be worthy of Dr. Sun Yat-sen.

Soviet Union Discovers Major Political Conspiracy: Attempt to Organize Fascist Groups, Many Foreign Nationals Arrested 53

(Moscow) The Soviet Union has discovered a large-scale conspiracy aimed at organizing a Fascist group, leading to Soviet police conducting extensive searches for conspirators throughout the country. According to official authorities, numerous foreign nationals have been arrested, including residents of German, Austrian, Swedish, Polish, and other nationalities. They are accused of propagating Fascist ideology and engaging in other activities detrimental to Soviet interests. A Berlin newspaper's Moscow correspondent telegraphed his office stating that the reason for the panic among the Soviet political police is currently unknown. However, besides Moscow, other locations in the Soviet Union are also taking precautionary measures. The correspondent further stated that five Germans are among those arrested. (Reuters, 11th)

Japanese Political Parties Oppose Military Interference in Politics 54

(Tokyo) Forty executives from the Seiyukai and Minseito parties' Diet groups held a joint discussion meeting on the afternoon of the 10th to exchange views on the current situation. They decided on the following slogans:

(1) Resolutely oppose reducing the authority of the Diet and deny any attempts at political manipulation.

(2) Repel active-duty military personnel from interfering in politics.

(3) Repel bureaucrats from exceeding their authority and engaging in conspiracies.

(4) We must urge the party executives to unite and uphold constitutional government. (Domei News Agency, 11th)

Germany Accelerates Warship Construction: Plans for Thirty-Eight Vessels of Various Sizes, Within the Limits Permitted by the Anglo-German Naval Agreement 55

(Berlin) It has recently been learned that Germany is rapidly advancing its naval construction to reach the level stipulated in the Anglo-German Naval Agreement, allowing Germany to have 35% of the British Navy's tonnage. It is reported that the warships currently under construction include: (1) One battleship of 35,000 tons; (2) One aircraft carrier of 19,000 tons; (3) Three cruisers of 10,000 tons; (4) Six destroyers; (5) Twelve torpedo boats; (6) Fourteen submarines. Furthermore, a battleship of 26,000 tons is being built in Kiel, a sister ship to the "Scharnhorst I," launched last month. (Reuters, 11th)

Litvinov's Speech: Soviet Union Self-Assured and Fearless, "Pot is Full, Not Afraid of Isolation," World Cannot Have Peace Without the Soviet Union 56

(Moscow) Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov's diplomatic achievements are outstanding, and the government has awarded him the highest-level Order of Lenin. Today, upon receiving the award, Litvinov stated that the Soviet Union is militarily superior to any enemy or coalition of enemies and therefore fears no isolation. He also knows that other countries cannot have peace without the Soviet Union; therefore, the isolation of the Soviet Union is not a problem. Other European countries, if isolated, will not be able to resist aggression. The Soviet Union can calmly wait for other countries to choose their path. (National Telegram, 10th)

(Moscow) Foreign Minister Litvinov firmly stated that the Soviet Union is determined to maintain peace and that there are only two policies in international relations: one is collective security, and the other is compromise with aggressors. One of these two must be chosen. The Soviet Union is now relying on its own strength within the country and observing which path Europe will take. However, the Soviet Union knows that other countries cannot achieve peace without the Soviet Union. He concluded by saying that the problem today is not isolating the Soviet Union but isolating European countries, making them unable to defend themselves and subjected to the trampling of aggressors. (Reuters, 10th)

(Moscow) The Presidium of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union held a meeting on the 10th of this month and awarded the Order of Lenin to People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs Litvinov. Upon receiving the medal, Litvinov gave a speech stating: "When I follow the instructions of our party leader, Stalin, and strive to do my best to benefit our great socialist motherland, I am also serving all of humanity. The reason is that bourgeois views often hold that diplomats are solely specialists in lying to protect their own country's interests, while the characteristic of Soviet diplomats is to always tell the truth, not only for the benefit of their own country but also for the benefit of all of humanity's workers. Soviet diplomacy is the struggle for peace, and peace is what all of humanity needs. The foundation of Soviet foreign policy is forever unchanging. In 1919, when I first went abroad on a Soviet diplomatic mission, my task was to propose peace to certain countries who were then attacking the Soviet Republic, attempting to interfere in its internal affairs and enslave its workers and peasants, just as certain countries are now mistreating Spain. At that time, proposing peace could be misunderstood as a sign of weakness, but we still proposed it. Now, this kind of misunderstanding will not happen again. The world has deeply believed in our country's inviolable power and infinite self-defense capabilities, but we still propose peace and constantly propose peace. When we participated in the first international conference, we proposed universal disarmament. Since then, even though our military strength has grown stronger day by day, our military industry and our fighting potential make us superior to any possible enemy, or the combined forces of many enemies, we still reiterate this proposal and reiterate it at every opportunity. Our armament is not to wage war with anyone, but to prevent others from having the desire to boldly try force with us. For the same purpose, we have proposed to all countries, one by one, the best system for organizing universal peace. I insist that it is universal because we not only hope that our country can enjoy peace but also that all of humanity can enjoy peace. Since our proposal for universal disarmament, which we have always regarded as the most important and indispensable guarantee of peace, was abandoned, we have proposed a system for guaranteeing peace, namely, treaties of non-aggression between neighboring countries, local pacts for collective defense against aggressors, the international definition of aggression, and the strengthening of international solidarity based on the League of Nations. Many journalists and politicians believe that this peace organization has already gone bankrupt, but this is completely false and is merely another official method of opposing peace. This organization has not yet been realized, and the struggle to have it accepted is still ongoing. How can one immediately say that it has already gone bankrupt? Currently, besides the Soviet Union, are there any other countries that have concluded non-aggression treaties with their neighbors? Even if there are, are they truly doing so in a spirit of peace, rather than using it as a means to frankly cover their rear and flanks for aggressive purposes? Our definition of aggression has so far only been accepted by our neighboring countries and has not been universally recognized internationally. When a member of the League of Nations recently attacked another member, we had to argue at the League of Nations that there was indeed an act of aggression, and this debate made the general measures against the aggressor numb. As for the concept of local pacts, it seems that most European countries have accepted it in theory. But where are these pacts? At the same time, the strengthening of the League of Nations, which most countries have vowed to support, has been delayed forever month after month and year after year under various pretexts, yielding no results. If one must speak of bankruptcy, then bankrupt are the policies of those countries that outwardly accept the Soviet Union's proposals, constantly declare their support for collective security, the indivisibility of peace, the stability of the principles of the League of Nations, and local pacts, but in reality, they are slacking off on these concepts. Bankrupt are the policies of those governments that believe that preparing to resist imminent aggression can only be carried out with the consent and participation of an aggressor who is known to all. Bankrupt are the policies of those governments that ignore violations of international treaties, ignore unquestionable acts of aggression, and instead flatter the perpetrators of these acts, catering to their will, hoping that they will be satisfied with their gains and declare, 'We will not commit any more crimes.' However, history has already told us that aggression and expansion never have a time of satisfaction. Every success, every concession obtained, will be used by the aggressor for new attacks. A policy of cowardly concessions to aggressors only emboldens them even more. Currently, the organization of collective security, the conclusion of regional pacts, and even joint diplomatic steps are all avoided, for fear that the aggressor will see this as forming a bloc. However, the aggressor himself sneers at this maliciously and forms his own bloc. Thus, those countries that previously claimed to be neutral arbiters also feel threatened and have to hastily arm themselves to avoid this danger. Whose policy is bankrupt, is it not clear? We have every reason to assume that many countries have begun to learn lessons from this bankruptcy. But the choices of routes are too few, there are only two: one is the Soviet Union's proposal for collective security, in which all peaceful countries organize a collective defense to resist the few and not-so-fearsome aggressors; the other is the route proposed by the aggressors and their agents in various countries, which has gained enthusiastic support, especially among medium-sized and small countries, namely, the so-called route of compromise with the aggressors, which is actually a compromise between the shrimp and the shark, hoping that the shark will not swallow them whole in one bite but will only nibble off a claw. Of course, at least not at the time of action. As for what we rely on, it is our own defense equipment. We can safely wait and see how Europe chooses. We firmly believe that if other countries are willing to organize true peace, guarantee collective security, and unite all peaceful forces to counter aggressive forces, it can only succeed with the Soviet Union's participation. Only the Soviet Union can build a barrier of peace in Europe. This is something that the aggressors themselves may also know deeply, and for this reason, they are doing their best to isolate Western Europe from the Soviet Union. But I must insist that the issue is not the isolation of the Soviet Union, but the isolation of other countries in Europe, making them defenseless against aggressors and forced to obey. The Soviet Union's diplomacy will be the same as before, still fighting for peace in the same way as before. The superiority of these methods has long been proven by daily lessons. As for myself, I will continue to perform my work in a Bolshevik manner, so that I can continue to live up to the honor conferred upon me today." (TASS, 10th)

Under the Cover of Airplanes and Artillery, Government Troops in Spain Launch Successful Counter-Offensive, Reinforcements Arrive from Catalonia Province, Morale of the Capital's Garrison Greatly Boosted 57

Madrid: Several battalions of reinforcements from Catalonia province arrived today, and, under the cover of airplanes and artillery, launched an offensive against the rebel positions in the southern suburbs. They have driven back the rebels from the former Royal Botanical Garden, and the rebel salient has been pushed back to its base in the western suburbs. (National Telegram, 11th)

Madrid: According to a public communiqué from the authorities here, government militia forces today launched a successful counter-offensive in the Casa de Campo area near the Royal Palace, forcing the enemy to retreat. Several airplanes participated in the battle to provide support. The militia forces continue to hold all bridgeheads across the Manzanares River. (Reuters, 11th)

Madrid: A special dispatch from our correspondent states that the Nationalist air force, which belongs to the National Army in the outskirts of Madrid, was particularly active yesterday. It is estimated that within twenty minutes, sixteen airplanes successively dropped bombs on the government army positions, with extremely intense force. The government army positions stretched for approximately five kilometers, and bombs fell like rain everywhere, with smoke and dust pervading the area. The entire city of Madrid was almost obscured by the smoke. At the same time, the Nationalist artillery batteries launched intensive artillery fire against the government army positions at the "Toledo" bridge and the "Segovia" bridge outside the south gate. However, the government army held the entire line and did not retreat at all. At 1:30 PM, they used artillery to heavily bombard the Nationalist positions in the town of Carabanchel in the southern suburbs, inflicting heavy damage. By 2:00 PM, the government troops' positions in the Casa de Campo Park in the western suburbs had also greatly improved. In addition, a unit of reinforcements dispatched from the Autonomous Region of Catalonia arrived in the capital at 4:00 PM, carrying a large number of new-style weapons. The military appearance was very impressive, and therefore, the authorities were greatly pleased, and the morale of the people was boosted. (Havas, 11th)

(London) According to a telegram from our special correspondent with the Spanish Nationalist army, a brigade of Moorish and foreign legion troops, commanded by Ambassador Gastón, has reportedly occupied the northern railway station in Madrid. This brigade reached its destination by crossing the King's Bridge from the Casa de Campo area near the Royal Palace. However, the main line of the Nationalist army is still limited to the west bank of the Manzanares River. Despite heavy artillery bombardment and air raids, the government militia forces continue to firmly defend all bridges and avenues leading to the bridges. The government forces' direct artillery batteries are very inactive, apparently due to a lack of ammunition. (Reuters, 11th)

Madrid Front Line: The rebels have today advanced to the vicinity of the old military palace in the northwest of the capital. The main battle is still taking place on the banks of the Manzanares River in the south. The rebel shock troops have penetrated deep into various parts of the city and are engaged in hand-to-hand combat with the government forces. The rebels' strategy today is to follow the old tactic of taking Irún, avoiding a rapid offensive and instead gradually encircling the city to avoid heavy losses. The government army is making every effort to strengthen its defensive line, which is a total of eight miles long and defended by approximately 50,000 troops. (National Telegram, 10th)

Madrid: Government officials recently issued a declaration stating, "We are now planning to add more airplanes, so that the skies of Madrid will be completely covered by aircraft wings. The residents will soon be able to witness this scene." The National Defense Committee is currently focusing on defense work and has gained the trust of the people, so its orders are obeyed without resistance. A total of four orders were issued today: (1) Residents who have not joined the militia and possess weapons must hand them over to the police station. (2) Troops should patrol all streets to help maintain order and should intervene when residents are assaulted. (3) Residents in each building should form committees, dispatch responsible personnel to search for concealed weapons in the buildings, and take turns guarding in front of the buildings. (4) Residents in each district should practice street fighting and dig trenches. In addition, the committee also distributed leaflets to instill various technical knowledge in the public, such as advising the public to prepare empty bottles, store them with kerosene, and when Nationalist tanks arrive, ignite the kerosene and throw it at them. (Havas, 11th)

Seville: General Driaño, Commander-in-Chief of the Nationalist army in the south, recently issued a broadcast message stating, "The failure to capture Madrid quickly has caused people around the world to become impatient, but this undertaking cannot be achieved overnight. In the past, the enemy's forces spread throughout the country, but now they are confined to a precarious city, still thinking of putting up a stubborn resistance. By comparing the past with the present, the outcome is clear. In order to avoid setbacks, our army has to take some preventive measures, such as consolidating the recovered areas, which is one aspect. The advance of modern armies is also a complex undertaking. Our army does not want to advance lightly for this reason. As far as yesterday's battle situation is concerned, our army's right wing on the Madrid front advanced one kilometer. The government army attacked our army's left wing but was repelled and suffered heavy losses." (Havas, 11th)

Defending the Precarious City, Vowing Not to Surrender

The authorities understand this, and they will not rashly abandon it. Given time, the government army will surely win. As for the Nationalist army, it does not have the strength to support its attacks, which are merely a show of force. Therefore, its collapse is imminent." This kind of atrocity is truly outrageous. (Havas, 10th)

Rebel Strategy: Avoiding Strength and Attacking Weakness

Talavera de la Reina (100 kilometers southwest of Madrid): A special dispatch from our correspondent states that the news released by the high-ranking military officials of the Nationalist army to the news reporters regarding the war situation in the outskirts of Madrid is extremely scarce. According to the general impression, in the past two days, the strategy adopted by the Nationalist army has been to find the weakest point in the enemy's defense line in order to avoid strength and attack weakness. Therefore, they sometimes attack and sometimes counter-attack, but have not achieved any substantial results. It has recently been reported that the government army launched an attack on the right wing of the Nationalist army near the village of Villaverde yesterday (southeast of Madrid, no more than six or seven kilometers from the city), but it failed and retreated in disarray. At the same time, the left wing of the Nationalist army made slight progress near the "Florida" bridge east of Casa de Campo Park in the western suburbs of Madrid. Apart from these two points, the front lines are still relatively calm. The Nationalist army is only carrying out mopping-up operations in the villages near Madrid that it occupied a few days ago, capturing many government officers and soldiers. (Havas, 10th)

Airplanes and Heavy Artillery Launch Fierce Bombardment

Madrid: Several airplanes belonging to the Nationalist army came to the city again at 3:00 PM today and dropped bombs. Airplanes belonging to the government army immediately took off to intercept them, and they finally drove away the enemy airplanes. At 5:00 PM, the heavy artillery batteries belonging to the Nationalist army began to bombard the city. Several shells often landed in the city, and the sound of explosions reverberated far and wide, causing people to tremble. The Havas News Agency's Spanish branch is only 50 meters away from the Congress of Deputies, separated only by a small square, so it was also greatly startled. It is said that the Nationalist army's use of heavy artillery seems to be aimed at disrupting the morale of government officials in the city of Madrid, so its shelling is mostly aimed at public institutions. Unfortunately, its aiming is not accurate and it failed to hit the targets, but it destroyed civilian residences, harming innocent people, resulting in many deaths and injuries. Italy, Austria, and Hungary: Three-Nation Conference Opens, Seeking Compromise on Three Issues; Italy Determined to Protect Austrian Independence 59

(Vienna) The foreign ministers' conference of Italy, Austria, and Hungary is scheduled to hold its first decisive meeting at 3:30 PM today, adjourning at 5:00 PM. Today marks the birthday of King Victor Emmanuel III of Italy. Austrian government representatives, along with personnel from the Italian and Hungarian delegations, attended a celebratory Mass at an Italian church this morning. Afterward, they jointly attended a luncheon hosted by Austrian President Miklas. The government will also host a grand banquet at the Hungarian Palais tonight, inviting members of the Italian and Hungarian delegations. It is expected that 1,500 guests will be invited to the banquet. (Havas, 11th)

(Rome) Regarding the issue of the Italy-Austria-Hungary foreign ministers' conference, the semi-official "Popolo di Roma" newspaper's Vienna correspondent, Signor Senureti, recently stated, "The three foreign ministers' conference should recognize Italy's annexation of Abyssinia in law." The three foreign ministers will also reach a compromise on the following three main issues: (1) the attitude to be adopted regarding the collective security system; (2) the issue of preventing Bolshevism and dealing with the situation in Spain; and (3) the issue of economic cooperation. Regarding the first issue, the three foreign ministers' conference should state that although Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant stipulates that "The Assembly may from time to time advise the reconsideration by Members of the League of treaties which have become inapplicable," the League of Nations has consistently failed to amend the various peace treaties after the European War for the past fifteen years. Therefore, any collective security system based on the League of Nations will inevitably lack power. However, Austria cannot explicitly oppose the principle of collective security for the time being and will continue to maintain its current attitude, which should also be recognized by the three foreign ministers' conference. Regarding the second issue, the three foreign ministers' conference should state that the three countries have completely identical interests in resisting communism and dealing with the Spanish Civil War, so they should take joint action. As for the third issue of economic cooperation, any of the three countries has the right to develop economic relations with other countries. This right, including Austria's planned trade agreement with Germany, should be recognized by the three foreign ministers' conference. In addition, the three foreign ministers' conference should reaffirm the following proposition: all countries that aspire to peace must unite around the Rome Protocols of Italy, Austria, and Hungary, as well as the agreements between Germany and Italy. As for the issue of treaty revision, the three foreign ministers' conference should state that treaty revision cannot be expected to be realized until the international atmosphere is cleared. To clear the international atmosphere, the influence of the Soviet Union on certain countries, such as Czechoslovakia, must be eliminated. (Havas, 11th)

(Paris) Regarding the Italy-Austria-Hungary foreign ministers' conference, "Le Journal" recently reported that, according to responsible sources, Italy may request the League of Nations to amend the Treaty of Trianon (i.e., the peace treaty with Hungary after the European War) in accordance with Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant, which stipulates that "The Assembly may from time to time advise the reconsideration by Members of the League of treaties which have become inapplicable." "Le Petit Journal" reported that the rumors that the Austrian Habsburg dynasty is about to be restored are mostly Italian air, used to test the opinions of various countries. According to the Rome correspondent of "Le Figaro", Italy should recognize Hungary's rearmament and some of its demands for the return of territory as legitimate and legal. (Havas, 11th)

(Vienna) Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano, who is on an official visit to Austria, solemnly assured Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg today that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is determined to protect Austrian independence. Austrian patriots were quite surprised by Ciano's recent discussions in Berlin and Mussolini's cold attitude towards Austria in his speech in Milan. Now that they have received this assurance from Ciano, they can rest assured. Ciano further hinted that Mussolini has sympathetically considered the restoration of Archduke Otto of the Habsburg dynasty, but does not intend to take active steps on this matter before the major Mediterranean issues are resolved. (Reuters, 10th)

Britain Guarantees Security, Actively Expanding Military, Navy Still the First Line of Defense, Air Force Striving to Surpass Other Countries 61

(London) Sir Inskip, Minister for Coordination of Defence, stated in the House of Commons this afternoon, when discussing the British national defense issue, that the navy is still the first line of defense, and that the army and air force should urgently cooperate. The main purpose of expanding the British air force is to defend Britain from the danger of air raids and to develop a strong air force to resist foreign enemies. This is the goal and aspiration of the British people. In terms of speed, capacity, and flight range, British aircraft are not inferior to other countries. Britain's national defense, in addition to the air force, is also perfected by other means, such as artillery, searchlights, and other technical equipment. Inskip also stated that the increase in British aircraft production has just begun and will continue to increase next year until 1940. The government aircraft factory in Nottingham will start shipping within six weeks. Powerful artillery is the most important thing in air defense. Inskip continued that army recruitment is progressing slowly, while navy and air force recruitment is doing well. There are 60,000 applicants for 20,000 places, and the number of pilots has increased by 50%. If Britain takes appropriate measures, he does not believe that war cannot be avoided. However, once Britain joins the war, it will never be able to stop until it obtains security. This means that Britain must make the greatest effort to seek complete victory. The British government has decided not to appoint a Minister of Supply. Unless there is strong evidence to prove that this appointment is necessary, the British government will study this matter periodically. The rearmament program has greatly strained the national finances. If the government intervenes in industries during peacetime, there is a danger of disrupting the national financial structure. He believes that the House of Commons will be very wise and have a broad vision to meet the needs of the country without stopping the export trade on which the country's financial position depends. Sir Hoare, the First Lord of the Admiralty, concluded the national defense debate, recalling that speakers in the House of Commons have never inquired about the seriousness of the situation or the need for rearmament, and said that any international disarmament discussions cannot start from the current situation, but must be discussed based on the appropriate level of security for the British Empire. Hoare denied the claim that the British air force program is lagging behind other countries and expressed satisfaction with the current state of the British air force, resolutely stating that as for the so-called "shadow industry," that is, several manufacturers each undertaking to build a component of an aircraft, when factories were first started to do this in a fair way, it was intended to continue issuing manufacturing tools so that in the event of an emergency, they could carry out all the procedures in one place. Although progress has been gradually made in national defense affairs, there is still much work to be done, such as some issues regarding supply that need to be studied. Hoare concluded by saying that we are deeply aware of the seriousness of the world situation and feel that it is urgent to speed up everything. (Reuters, 10th)

Britain Mass-Producing Bulletproof Shelters, Each Costing £150, Private Purchases Available on Installments 62

(London) Private families can now purchase bomb shelters for home use on an installment plan. This is the latest British invention to protect the lives of citizens in future air raids. There are now many trading houses established, specializing in the manufacture of these shelters and the supply of their various equipment. The first shelter to be advertised is called "Igro." It is reported that the manufacturing cost of this shelter is quite high, because the United Dominions Trust Company, a well-known London financial institution, has provided funding, so the price can be paid in installments. Proceedings of the 17th League of Nations Assembly 68

1. The question of the credentials of the Abyssinian delegation… Work of the Chinese delegation in various committees (A) First Committee (B) Second Committee (C) Third Committee (D) Fourth Committee (E) Fifth Committee (F) Sixth Committee… 3. The question of the reorganization of the League of Nations Covenant… 4. Speech of the Chinese delegate in the general discussion of the Assembly… 5. Process of China’s election as a member of the Administrative Council and a judge of the Hague Court… 6. Conclusion…

Geneva Correspondence. The annual general assembly of the League of Nations (the 17th) began on September 21st and adjourned on October 11th this year. This major assembly had several issues worth reporting, and it can be said to be a relatively successful one in recent years under the tense world situation. First, such as the question of the qualifications of the Abyssinian representative, viewers felt that it was a difficult obstacle for the League of Nations a few days before the League of Nations Assembly. No matter what method the Assembly took to refuse the participation of the Abyssinian country in the Assembly, it could not maintain the world's public's final belief in it in terms of law and morality. Although there were several reasons for the vote of the Abyssinian country to participate in the Assembly this time, it cannot be said that it was not a victory between public opinion and the threat of power. From this point of view, the belief of the world's people in the League of Nations can still be preserved for a while. Second, the Administrative Council has returned to normal. From the general purpose of the League of Nations, the Administrative Council has shown an unbalanced state since Japan withdrew from the League and China failed to be elected. The Administrative Council only has European and American representatives, but lacks Asia, which not only violates the spirit of the Covenant, but also is an important obstacle to international cooperation. This regret has now been made up. Third, the disarmament conference, which the world's people eagerly anticipated, has been in decline for several years, and now there is hope of revival. In addition, regarding the reorganization of the League of Nations Covenant, although the future result is still difficult to guess, judging from the opinions of more than 30 countries that have already responded, the majority advocate strengthening the power of the Covenant, tending towards practicality. If the world's people do not give up their supervisory power, world peace may not be hopeless. As one of the members, China has a mission of peace in the world no less than any other country in terms of population and region. China's participation in the work of the League of Nations is not only for its own sake, but also for world peace. We not only hope for international understanding, but also hope that our own people will understand. The reporter hereby reports the process of this conference, fearing that the length is too long, and because of time constraints, the description inevitably focuses on our country, but issues such as the reorganization of the League of Nations and disarmament are described in summary for the reference of those who study international issues.

An Abyssinian Delegate 69

The Twists and Turns of Qualification: Before discussing this issue, a related question must be revisited. This concerns the League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol's trip to Rome. This decisive trip provoked much criticism from public opinion. Some said Avenol's visit to Rome was less about urging and more about apologizing. Regardless, we don't need to concern ourselves with that. However, at a minimum, an informal opinion seemed to have formed regarding the issue of Abyssinian delegates attending the General Assembly. If we haven't misinterpreted this opinion, then the reason why the Italian delegation later waited on the border before departing for Geneva doesn't need explanation. This is a question that many still have. Perhaps only Avenol can answer it. Under this question, many twists and turns arose, resulting in the first ever difficulty in forming a Credentials Committee in the history of the League of Nations. Small countries, wanting to please everyone, couldn't bear this significant responsibility. Large countries like Britain and France, while having their fixed foreign policies, hoped to use this decisive opportunity to bring Italy back to Geneva, to facilitate the Locarno issue. However, legally, they couldn't find a sufficient reason to revoke Abyssinia's membership in the League of Nations. They were also unwilling to openly shoulder the responsibility under the public scrutiny of the world. Therefore, under these circumstances, the Credentials Committee couldn't be formed, and a voting method had to be used to resolve the issue. As a result of the voting, representatives from Britain (Eden), France (Foreign Minister Delbos), the Soviet Union (Litvinov), Czechoslovakia (Osuský), Greece (Politis), Turkey (Aras), Peru (Dudela), New Zealand (Jordan), and the Netherlands (Limburg) were elected. Thus, the Credentials Committee was finally established. Our country wasn't elected, and some in our delegation were quite gleeful. However, if the same event occurred in our Executive Yuan after our election, what attitude would our country adopt?

The committee could only complete its report on the third day after the General Assembly convened. Several meetings were held in between, and it was almost impossible to find a concrete solution. Consequently, the committee created a subcommittee to specifically study Abyssinia's current situation and the legal qualifications of its leader, and then report back to the committee for discussion. Fortunately, there were two relatively courageous representatives on the committee, one was the Dutch representative Limburg, and the other was the Soviet representative Litvinov. Limburg suggested seeking the opinion of the Hague Court, which, although a way of shirking responsibility, was much more superior than a policy of trying to please everyone. After the committee discussed this proposal, two concerns were discovered. First, there was a fear that after the court studied the issue, it would consider it not a purely legal question, but an international political issue, and decline the responsibility of advising. Second, due to time constraints, the court's response couldn't be obtained in the short term, and at least several weeks would be needed. Distant water couldn't quench the immediate thirst. The General Assembly couldn't wait for the court's response before proceeding with its work. Finally, Litvinov said very emotionally that if anyone opposed Abyssinia's participation in the General Assembly, please formally state the reasons. If there wasn't a committee, why delay any further? As a result, everyone looked at each other, but no one dared to openly object. The qualifications of the Abyssinian representative could then be approved. Although it was unfortunate for Eden and Delbos, it couldn't be said to be unfortunate for the League of Nations. Many British and French newspapers said that Litvinov had achieved a great victory. The British Conservative Party's official newspaper condemned Eden, saying that he hadn't implemented his foreign policy. Even the Labour Party's newspaper said that Eden had reached the point of resigning, and asked why he hadn't resigned yet. It can be seen that this twist was not a temporary occurrence, but merely a temporary change. The reasons in the report were as follows: "Upon examination of the credentials, it was found that they were from the same authority that had previously dispatched delegation to attend the General Assembly several times. However, when the credentials were issued on the fourteenth and nineteenth of September (this year), Abyssinia's situation had undergone great changes in all aspects. The head of state was residing in a foreign government and was no longer in the capital. According to various documents, another government authority was to be established in another part of the country. It seems particularly difficult to judge the authority of that authority and the nature and scope of its power in relation to its head of state. The question itself lies in whether the mandate required by the head of state's legal title is entirely in accordance with the procedure. The Committee feels the seriousness of this issue, so no one has proposed taking a rejection approach, declaring the mandate unreasonable. On the contrary, no one is without doubt as to whether the procedure is followed. Under these circumstances, one might think of asking the General Assembly for the advice of the International Court, whether the credentials issued in the current position of His Majesty Haile Selassie meet the requirements of Article 5, Section 2 of the General Assembly's constitution, so that the bearer of the item is in accordance with Article 3, Section 1 of the covenant, as a representative of a member state of the League of Nations, but at the same time, another problem arises. If the court begins to discuss the above points, it is unlikely that an answer can be obtained within a few weeks. In that special period, the current General Assembly will inevitably be closed. At the same time, what status will the Abyssinian delegation be in? According to Article 5, Section 4 of the General Assembly's Constitution, "For any representative who has a disagreement, if the General Assembly has no other resolution, he may temporarily participate in the General Assembly and enjoy the same rights as other representatives." From the observation of this article, the question of whether the Abyssinian delegation can participate in the current General Assembly should be practically decided before the court's reply. The reason is very obvious. If the meaning of the last section is followed, the answer from The Hague will be of no practical value. Therefore, the best way is to ask the General Assembly to consider the Abyssinian delegation's credentials, regardless of whether they are reasonable or not, to be sufficient reason to allow its delegation to participate in the current General Assembly. This is the unanimous view of the Committee, and has been carefully considered when passing it, and it is believed that only by giving the delegation special assistance in the midst of doubts, and in terms of the current situation in Abyssinia, the measure is limited to the current General Assembly and does not involve any future opinions. Based on the above opinions and the implementation of its full responsibilities, the Committee respectfully requests the General Assembly to allow the Abyssinian delegation to participate in the work of the current General Assembly." After the report was read in the General Assembly, the Hungarian representative requested a vote, and the representatives from Austria and Albania seconded. The General Assembly then voted, with thirty-nine countries voting in favor of the report, including the South African Federation, Argentina, Australia, Belgium, Britain, Canada, China, Colombia, Cuba, Denmark, the Dominican Republic, Spain, Estonia, Abyssinia, Finland, France, Greece, Haiti, India, Iraq, Iran, Ireland, Latvia, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Mexico, Norway, New Zealand, the Netherlands, Peru, Poland, Romania, Sweden, Czechoslovakia, Turkey, the Soviet Union, Uruguay, and Yugoslavia. Four countries voted against, including Albania, Austria, Hungary, and Ecuador. Six countries abstained, including Bulgaria, Panama, Portugal, Siam, Switzerland, and Venezuela. The report was then passed. Abyssinia was able to participate in the current General Assembly, and the appearance of this twist, as stated in the committee's report, was due to the king's departure and the government not being in the capital, which was equivalent to losing the qualifications of a member state. However, no explanation was given as to why the king left and why the government wasn't in the capital. The invaded party lost all rights, which can serve as a lesson. The day before the report was completed, the chairman of the International Wireless Radio Peace Propaganda Conference, which was being held at the same time as the League of Nations, announced his withdrawal from the conference on the orders of his government, to express a threat to the League of Nations. The Italian delegation waiting for news on the border had no choice but to drive back to Rome. The black-shirted prime minister's heart was naturally very uncomfortable. (To be continued)

Shao Yuan Chong’s Impressions of Guangxi: The People's Organizations Are Sound, Women Are Hardworking and Bear Heavy Burdens, The Army Is Organized Into Seven Divisions, and the Militia Has Mostly Resumed Training, The Central and Local Authorities Jointly Reorganize the Currency System 70

Hankou Correspondence: Shao Yuan Chong, a member of the Central Committee of the Kuomintang, went to Guangdong earlier this month to attend Chairman Hu's state funeral and toured Guangxi. He has now completed his tasks and traveled north from Guangzhou through Guangxi by car. On the morning of the 9th, he took a car from Hengyang to Changsha. That evening, around 8 o'clock, he took a train to Hankou, arriving at Xujiapeng Station at 8 a.m. on the 10th. He crossed the river and stayed at the Pacific Hotel. In the evening, he attended a joint banquet hosted by the Pacification Headquarters and the two party branches of the province and city. He was scheduled to pay respects to Yang Yongtai on the 11th and give speeches at the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. He left Hankou by steamer that night to return to Nanjing. Shao shared his impressions of his Guangxi tour, saying that although his visit to Guangxi lasted only eight days, what he saw in various aspects was very pleasant and what impressed him the most was the soundness of the people's organizations and the hardworking and burden-bearing nature of women. The people's organization in the province is headed by the village chief, who also serves as the principal of the people's school and the head of the militia. With the power concentrated, it is easier to handle affairs. Most of the village chiefs have received considerable training and can handle affairs with a spirit of hard work. Currently, the number of militias in the province is around one million. In general, women can bear heavy burdens and are not only responsible for most of the agricultural work, but also for hard work such as carrying water and sedan chairs. The Guangxi reconstruction work has now been completed two-thirds. Initially, more than 300,000 militiamen were mobilized, and now more than 200,000 have been demobilized. Because the people's organizations are sound, mobilization is easy and demobilization is not difficult. The Guangxi army is currently organized into six divisions, and the 19th Route Army was recently organized into one division, for a total of seven divisions. Mr. Bai Jiansheng is currently working hard on the demobilization of the army, and his departure date to the north has not yet been determined, but it will be after the demobilization work is completed. In short, Guangxi is now working hard from top to bottom. Although the financial situation is not very affluent, the authorities are dealing with it effectively, so several important tasks in recent years have a good foundation. Looking back at Guangdong Province, although the financial situation has been more affluent than Guangxi in the past few years, all important tasks, such as people's organizations, are far less developed than in Guangxi. From this, it can be seen that things depend on people. As long as you can work hard, you will have satisfactory results. At present, Guangxi's currency is still mainly circulated in the form of Guangxi Bank banknotes. Its exchange rate to the central government's banknotes is only about 50 cents per yuan, so the work of reorganizing the currency system is extremely important. The Guangxi Provincial Government and the central government are currently working hard on this task. Shao also said that Guangdong Province is currently engaged in production construction and financial reorganization. After the completion of the Yuehan Railway, the north and south are connected, and Guangdong's prosperity will be even more advanced. However, after the opening of the railway, unfortunate incidents have occurred one after another, and the road infrastructure seems to be not yet perfect and the speed is very slow. The cleanliness of the vehicles needs to be improved and should be rectified as soon as possible."

The National Private Electricity Industry Association Holds its Eighth Annual Meeting in Nanjing, Over a Thousand Representatives Attended, Re-election of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members 71

Nanjing Correspondence: The National Private Electricity Industry Association held its eighth annual meeting at the Central Hotel in Nanjing on the morning of the first. Over a thousand representatives from electrical companies in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Fujian, Hubei, Hunan, Sichuan, Shandong, Henan, Chahar, Suiyuan, Guangdong, and other provinces, as well as electrical equipment manufacturers in Beijing and Tianjin, attended. After the formalities were completed, Chairman Wang Shucheng, and representatives from the Construction Committee of the Central Party Department, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of the Interior, the Ministry of Communications, the Nanjing Municipal Government, and the New Life Movement General Association gave speeches. Guests Xu Enzeng and Zhuang Zhihuan gave speeches, and Shen Sifang gave a thank you speech. In the afternoon, a members' meeting was held, where various business regulations were discussed. In the evening, a banquet was hosted by the Shanghai Siemens Electrical Factory, and guests performed martial arts, Peking opera, movies, and other entertainment. On the morning of the 2nd, the executive and supervisory committee members were re-elected. As a result, the Hankou Jiji Water and Electricity Company, the Zhenjiang Da Zhao Electric Company, the Wuxian Suzhou Electric Company, the Fujian Fuzhou Electric Company, the Huzhou Wuxing Electric Company, the Wuhu Mingyuan Electric Company, the Shaoxing Daming Electric Company, the Shanghai Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, the Beiping Huashang Electric Light Company, the Shandong Jinan Electric Company, the Ningbo Yongyao Electric Company, the Shanghai Pudong Electric Company, the Shanghai Huashang Electric Company, the Changsha Hunan Electric Light Company, the Changzhou Wujin Electric Factory, the Jiangdu Zhenyang Electric Company, and the Chengdu Qiming Electric Light Company were elected as executive committee members. The Fujian Xiamen Electric Power Company, the Jiangsu Changshu Electric Factory, the Wenzhou Puhua Electric Company, the Hubei Hanyang Electric Company, the Pinghu Minghua Electric Company, the Zhengzhou Mingyuan Electric Light Company, the Shanghai Xianghua Electric Light Company, the Taiyuan Xinji Electric Light Company, and the Kaifeng Pulin Electric Light Company were elected as supervisory committee members. Wang Shucheng of the Hankou Jiji Company was elected as the standing chairman, Weng You of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company was elected as the standing vice chairman, and Shen Sifang of the Wuhu Mingyuan Company, Guo Zhicheng of the Zhenjiang Ren Zhao Company, Ding Chunzhi of the Suzhou Leiqi Factory, Liu Ya of the Fuzhou Electric Company, and Liu Chongyou of the Beiping Huashang Company were elected as standing committee members. In the afternoon, the Shanghai Yapp Electric Factory, Huatong Manufacturing Factory, and Huasheng Electric Factory hosted a banquet at the Pacific Hotel. In the afternoon, the Construction Committee invited members to visit the Electric Industry Testing Institute and the Electric Industry Personnel Training Class. In the evening, at the invitation of Director Pan and Chief Engineer Lu of the Capital Electric Power Plant, they went to visit and held a banquet at the International Club. On the morning of the 3rd, they visited the Yongli Chemical Industry Company in Pukou. In the afternoon, they visited the Power and Telecommunications Testing Laboratory and the Electric Machinery Manufacturing Room of the Central University. The conference closed on the morning of the 4th. The standing committee members, including Shu Cheng, Weng Yusan, Shen Sifang, and Guo Zhicheng, went to the National Economic Construction Movement General Association to state the difficulties faced by electric plants in various places and requested assistance and guidance, which was forwarded for review and approval. In the afternoon, the representatives were divided into groups to visit the Mausoleum of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, Wuzhou Park, Zijin Mountain, and Tangshan, and a portion of the representatives went to Wuhu to visit the Mingyuan Electric Company and tour the famous scenic spots of Caishiji, Fuyi, Yijishan, and Zheshan.

Songjiang: Results of Bone Steaming and Examination 72

Shi, wife of Sun Dexian of Wengjiao, Xinzhuang, suffered from mental illness. She hanged herself on August 14th of this year. After the coffin was prepared, someone, using a false name, filed lawsuits with courts at all levels, alleging that Shi was beaten by her husband and forced to commit suicide. The District Court and the High Court both dismissed the case. Another lawsuit was filed with the Supreme Court under the name Wang Liusheng. The court ordered the Songjiang Court to steam the bones in the coffin and conduct an examination. The High Court sent inspectors Xuan Fang and Yang Haiyang to Songjiang. On the afternoon of the 10th, the coffin was placed in the public forest clearing north of the North Gate. Chief Prosecutor Zhu presided over the examination, removed the bottom of the coffin, took out the body, removed the burial clothes, and according to the law, dissected the bones and tagged and sealed them one by one. Starting at 8 a.m. on the 11th, the bones were washed clean one by one and steamed. The examination revealed that she had hanged herself before death. The bones were packed in boxes, tagged, and sealed, and stored in the court for safekeeping, pending review by the Supreme Court. The coroner and others were dismissed.

Suzhou: Establishment of Demonstration Fields at Agricultural School 73

The Suzhou Agricultural School in Xiajin Bridge, in view of the great need for high-quality rice seeds in various places, decided to select more than ten farm families in the villages near the school to establish demonstration farmland, and actively guide them. After the harvest, they will buy as much as possible as material for large-scale promotion, and use roving guidance methods to gradually popularize them in various villages. Fifteen measures have been formulated and work is underway.

Zhou Pingda's Appeal Judgement 74

Zhou Pingda, the head of the Shanghai Zhenru Public Security Branch, and employees Xing Guonong and others were previously accused of causing death by torture of criminal suspects and were sentenced to imprisonment by the Shanghai District Court. Zhou Pingda and others appealed the original judgment to the High Court. After several trials, the case has now been concluded. Yesterday's judgment dismissed the portions of the original judgment concerning the crimes and sentences of Zhou Pingda and Xing Guonong. Zhou Pingda and Xing Guonong were found not guilty. The part of the attached civil lawsuit concerning compensation was also appealed to the decision, and the original judgment was revoked.

Banning Gambling Amidst Abundant Rice Harvest 75

Gambling has recently resurfaced in various parts of Wuxian County, with the urban area being the worst. County Magistrate Deng Xianghai, in view of the abundant autumn harvest this year, believes that if gambling is not strictly prohibited, it will be extremely harmful to the local communities. Therefore, he has specially formulated eight measures to prohibit gambling and submitted them to the Administrative Commissioner's Office for approval. They were announced on the 11th.

Wuxi: Commissioner's Office Holds Two Meetings 76

In order to effectively promote the construction of each county and handle the liaison work for controlling rice stem borers, the Second District Administrative Commissioner's Office convened two meetings on the morning of the 10th, one on construction and one on controlling rice stem borers. More than 20 people attended, including the county magistrates, heads of construction bureaus, section chiefs, and agricultural management personnel. Resolutions were passed on the following cases: (1) The implementation procedures for afforestation in each county in the 25th year of the Republic, in order to develop the forest industry and expand production. (2) Principles for regulating the winter rice stem borer control liaison methods in each county in the district to facilitate implementation. The date for rice stem borer control propaganda was set from November 14th to the 20th. Farmers were required to burn rice straw by the Qingming Festival next year, and the overall inspection date was set from January 20th to January 20th. The meeting adjourned at 12:30 p.m.

County Chamber of Commerce General Meeting 77

The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce convened its annual general meeting of members yesterday afternoon. 149 representatives attended, and the county government and county party branch sent personnel to attend for supervision and guidance. The following key cases were resolved: (1) The Foreign Goods Industry Association requested a reduction in business tax, still collected at 8 per thousand. (2) The Gold and Silver Industry Association proposed that the business tax be changed to 15 per thousand, requesting that it still be collected at the original 10 per thousand. The above two cases were discussed together and resolved that the chamber would submit them separately to the Finance Department for review and reduction. (3) It was proposed that the bank's small coins and auxiliary currency cannot be exchanged at any time, and that there are no exchange offices, requesting a discussion of relief measures. Resolved that those with exchange offices should be transferred to the Banking Association to request immediate exchange. Those without exchange offices will be reported to the department for instructions. (4) It was proposed that there is a special type of business that specializes in trading empty sales at the stock exchange as an improper business, and the authorities should strictly ban it. In addition, each industry often has price reductions and competitive sales, deliberately causing trouble, requesting the formulation of disposal methods. Resolved that special stores with illegitimate businesses should be strictly prohibited by the authorities. Price reductions and competitive sales in various industries involve industry rules, and each trade association should formulate its own methods and report them to the association for handling. (5) The brewing and other 14 industry associations stated that the association's expenses should be collected in accordance with Article 41 of the Commercial Association's regulations, based on the amount of capital of each industry, in order to equalize the burden. Resolved that each industry association should first investigate the capital of its members, and then the matter should be resolved by a temporary general meeting of members.

Yangzhou: Building a Dam to Block Shipping 78

The Huai River Waterways Commission will take advantage of the low water level in the canal to build the Shaobo dam to block and divert water in order to raise the water level and open the ship locks. Work is scheduled to start on the 12th. Small steamers will be temporarily prohibited from navigating between the 15th and 25th to avoid hindering the dam construction. On the 10th, the Jiangdu and Gaoyou county governments received the aforementioned instructions and forwarded them to the various shipping companies and relevant teams for reference.

Planning to Establish Township Telephones 79

The Jiangdu County Government believes that the county's telephone service has not yet reached all towns, and it is difficult to order the township chiefs in each district in case of emergency, and the public security bureaus stationed in each township also lack a method of rapid delivery of orders in case of emergency. Now that it is winter defense season, it is even more necessary to universally install telephones. On the 10th, the Construction Bureau Director Shu Guohua was ordered to make proper plans and report how to install them for approval.

Public Security Bureau Increases Inspection Shifts 80

Zhang Jinkui, Director of the Jiangdu Public Security Bureau, believes that the winter defense season requires strict precautions. He has strictly regulated the inspection methods. In addition to the outside officers and chiefs intensifying the inspection tasks and ordering them to be strictly implemented, he also assigned inside office personnel to participate in the night shift inspection work, with four people taking shifts each night to prevent negligence. This has been implemented since the evening of the 9th.

Nantong: Thorough Investigation of Embezzled Stolen Money 81

The Tongyi Xiesheng Flower Shop's flower collection banknotes of 15,000 yuan were robbed by bandits at Jiujiaba. The Public Security Bureau's Investigation Team tracked down and captured the bandit Li Youen and found 2,680 yuan of the original stolen money. The Fourth District Commissioner's Office discovered that the amount of stolen money recovered was more than this and detained the Investigation Team Leader Yao Dangping and Patrol Chief Zhao Jingui. They were transferred to the court on the previous day. After interrogation by Prosecutor Liu, they were both taken into custody at the detention center.

Haizhou: District Chief Pleads for Disaster Relief 82

The Fifth District Office of Muyang County reported that the district suffered a terrible yellow flood last year, and between July and August this year, due to the low-lying terrain, continuous rain caused a disaster, so that Datong, Qiaoliheng, Huangjiadang, Pangoudang and other villages had empty houses, and families were destitute. Winter is approaching, and they are suffering from hunger and cold. If relief is not provided immediately, they may become bandits or die in the gutters. The district chief Jiang Dounan, seeing this, telegraphed the county government and the county party branch yesterday, requesting them to report the situation to the province and various charitable organizations to allocate funds for relief to save them. It is said that the county government has reported this separately.

Ningbo: Handling Coastal Salt Fields 83

The Fenghua Salt Field Official Property Office, since receiving the provincial order to abolish it, transferred it to the county government for filing and continued handling. Because there are still quite a few barren and mature salt fields along the rivers and coast, and although the official properties in the city and countryside have been disposed of one after another, some are still in use, or are still occupied by the people, which should be investigated and disposed of according to regulations in order to determine property rights and increase income. Yesterday, a notice was issued stating that if anyone occupies salt fields or official properties, they must come to the county to report and receive them in order to survey and evaluate the price. Those who dare to delay will be auctioned off in accordance with the regulations.

Bandits Plunder and Injure People 84

Xu Li, a widow from Litonggang, Cizhong, is 36 years old and has only one nine-year-old son. Mother and son depend on each other for survival. At 6 a.m. on the 8th, two bandits suddenly broke into her home. Shi was cooking in the kitchen upstairs. After the two bandits went upstairs, they were about to open the box and search when Shi heard the sound and went upstairs. The bandits saw that there were no men in her house and immediately pressed her to the ground. One of them reached out and took off her lower clothes, intending to rape her. Seeing that the situation was not good, Shi shouted for help. The bandit, seeing that the good deed was difficult to accomplish, held a grudge and stabbed her head, face, arms and other parts with a sharp blade. At this time, neighbors had heard the call and rushed to gather, and arrested a bandit named Zhu Xiaozhong, and sent him to the Hongtang Public Security Bureau for further investigation. However, Shi was severely injured and may be in danger of death. The bandit named Agou has not yet been apprehended. The county government has ordered the investigation to be carried out.

Special Edition for the 6th Anniversary of the Ant Society

Our Beliefs (In Lieu of a Launching Statement) 85

The Ant Society has been established for six years now. Examining the achievements of our work over the past six years, what we have contributed to society and culture is truly very meager, and we cannot help but feel deeply ashamed. However, we are determined not to be discouraged. We believe that as long as we have a true understanding of culture and strive along the right path, our efforts will never be in vain, and we will gain some harvest.

We are not cultural supremacists. We oppose blaming all irrationality on culture, or using culture to solve everything. However, we will never deny the power of culture, and thus ignore its feedback effect on society. This is the reason why we are engaged in cultural movements.

We believe that culture, like everything else in the universe, is constantly flowing. Therefore, each era has its own culture. The culture of the past can no longer meet the needs of the present. Modern culture must be compatible with the needs of the present. This is our understanding of culture when we engage in cultural movements.

We oppose culture being monopolized by a small number of people and used as a tool to oppress the majority. We firmly advocate that culture should belong to the masses, it should be the spiritual food of the masses, and it should be used to improve the lives of the masses. Therefore, the masses are the target of our cultural movement.

Because the masses are the target of our cultural movement, we recognize that engaging in cultural movements must go deep into the masses, understand the needs of the masses, and use them as the guidelines for our cultural movement. This is the attitude we take towards cultural movements.

We believe that in the process of cultural development, the conflict between new and old cultures is an inevitable phenomenon. We must strive for the new culture, we must be unyielding, consistent from beginning to end, in order to fulfill our hopes. This is the spirit we should have towards cultural movements.

The above are the common beliefs of all members of the Ant Society. In the past, we worked hard under this common belief. It is still the case now. What about the future? We must adhere to this belief. The Ant Society is not only the Ant Society of the members of the Ant Society. The Ant Society should belong to the whole society. We deeply hope that people who are enthusiastic about cultural movements will give us valuable assistance.

Lyrics of the Ant Society Song 86

Ants are small insects that love group cooperation and mutual assistance,

Ants are a mass with a group organization,

We are all ants,

Not stupid worms that eat books and are useless,

In this trench where light and darkness duel,

We must rush forward,

Forward, forward, forward, forward, forward,

We must all rush forward,

With the spirit of ants,

To sow the seeds of new culture,

To make the light of the new world more brilliant and bright red,

Arise, arise, ants,

Everyone arise, ants,

Go forward to be the pioneers of freedom and equality, freedom and equality.

The Ant Society and the Current Stage of Cultural Movement 87

— Chen Zhuo

The current stage of the cultural movement is, of course, inherited from the previous stage. However, because of the continuous invasion of the enemy and the increasing national crisis, it must inevitably shoulder new tasks. What are these new tasks? It is to quickly establish a national defense culture. In other words: the current stage of the cultural movement should be the national defense cultural movement.

The national defense cultural movement, like the military, political, and economic national defense movements, is to gather the entire strength to resist the enemy's general attack, so that the national crisis can be saved and the final victory can be achieved.

This places an even greater responsibility on all cultural movement groups and individuals to promote it.

The Ant Society is a group that has always worked hard in cultural movements. In every period, it has shown great strength. This can be seen from its various departments. The continuous expansion of the Ant Library, the frequent performances of meaningful dramas by the Ant Drama Troupe, the expansion of the Ant Supplementary Night School, the change of the reading club to an academic research association, the holding of various friendships by the friendship association, and other various advances have not only made the number of members increase sharply every year, but also expanded the cultural impact day by day. On the one hand, this is due to the efforts of the members in the work of the various departments, but on the other hand, it cannot be said that it has grasped the tasks of each period.

Now that new tasks are in front of us, we must not only embrace the consistent spirit, but also redouble our efforts to join hands with all cultural movement groups, and hope that people who are enthusiastic about cultural movements will participate with us. Let us all move towards the current stage of cultural movement!

Chronicle of the Ant Society 94

Date The beginning of initiating and organizing this society was like this. At that time, there were several like-minded people who often gathered together to talk about life issues. In the end, everyone felt that this was not enough. On the one hand, they should pay attention to personal cultivation; on the other hand, we should pay more attention to the improvement of society. Therefore, these people began to initiate the organization of the Ant Society.

20.1.3 The first discussion meeting was held in Fudeli, Baoshan Road, and the name of the group was decided to be "Ant Society." A total of eight people signed the initiation, and it was decided that regular meetings would be held once a month, and the eight people would take turns convening (that is, the prototype of the current Friendship Association)

Yesterday's Armistice Day The British, American, French and Foreign Nationals Held a Special Ceremony The French Ambassador Nazia Inspects the Garrison 95

Yesterday (November 11) was Armistice Day. The participating military personnel and civilians from the British, American, and French communities in Shanghai held a special memorial ceremony. At 8:30 in the morning, they gathered in front of the Peace Statue on the Bund of Edward Road, knelt and paid respects. Consuls general from various countries participated. Then, at 10:45, a prayer service was held in the Red Church on Jiangxi Road. The British Aviation Association and the Qiluo General Association held tea parties in the afternoon. At 8:00 in the evening, veterans from various countries held a dinner at the French General Association on Myers Road. At 9:15, a music concert was held at the Lyceum Theatre on Baoshi Road.

French Community Commemoration

The French community in Shanghai enthusiastically celebrated Armistice Day yesterday. French Ambassador Nazia personally came to Shanghai to preside over the celebration. At 8:45 in the morning, a grand military parade was held in Gujiazhai Park. The participating troops included the French garrison in Shanghai and the French police guard. The ceremony was extremely grand. At 9:45, a Mass was held in St. Joseph's Church on Tianzhu Church Street to pray for peace. At 10:45, they went to the French Cemetery on Weimar Road to lay flowers. In the evening, a public banquet was held by the Veterans Friendship Association at the French General Association on Myers Road. The details are as follows:

Ambassador Inspects Troops

Yesterday morning at 8:45, French Ambassador Nazia inspected the garrison police in Gujiazhai Park. The participating troops were introduced by Defense Commander Lieutenant Colonel Belmaud and French Concession Police Chief Major Faber. The participating troops included a naval team, the 2nd Battalion of the 16th Colonial Infantry Regiment, a volunteer team, a tank team, recipients of military medals, and a delegation of volunteers (the above troops were commanded by Major Dutter), four police guard teams, a motorcycle team, a reserve team, a bicycle team, and a Russian patrol team (the above troops were commanded by Mr. Geber, Deputy Director of the French Concession Police Department). During the inspection, Mr. Nazia awarded medals to the following personnel: (A) Those who received medals from the garrison: Captain Le Belaur, French Legion of Honor Lieutenant Duru, French Legion of Honor Sergeant Hadong, Military Medal Sergeant Gu Lin, Military Medal Private Ji Silai, Military Medal (B) Those who received medals from the police: Western Police Binari, Municipal Council Medal (Note that this Western Police went to the scene of a robbery immediately after hearing the police siren, and after exchanging gunfire with the two robbers being pursued, he knocked down one of the two robbers and arrested the other) Yue Police Zhengmu Ruan Jiaduan (awarded the Annam Second Class Silver Medal of Honor) Yue Police Zhengmu Ruan Huijing (same as above) Yue Police Deputy Mu Ruan Wenmian (same as above) Yue Police Ruan Wenju (same as above)

French Ambassador Inspects Troops

Church Mass

At 9:45 in the morning, a grand Mass was held in St. Joseph's Church on Tianzhu Church Street to commemorate the French who died in the European city. French Ambassador Nazia, French Consul General Bopais, Defense Commander Lieutenant Colonel Belati, French Concession Police Chief Major Faber, French Liaison Ship Daer Captain Qiao, French Municipal Council Supervisor Wei Zhiren, and various directors, as well as French Public Works Bureau police officers, and many French nationals, all participated in the ceremony.
