Movies

Robert Taylor Meets Audience in "Nanjing" 220

Robert Taylor, the ideal lover in the hearts of women who has been in the film industry for only a few years, is meeting the Shanghai audience again from today in the blockbuster "政海巾幗" (State of the Union) publicly screened at the Nanjing Grand Theater. He is paired with Hollywood's glamorous star Joan Crawford. She plays a smart and capable woman in the film, relying on her far-sighted mind and extraordinary thinking, which is enough to influence the political situation of President Jackson's era in the United States at that time. In addition, the scenes of love between men and women are added, which makes it more vivid, lively, and intriguing. In order to produce this film, MGM not only paid attention to the exquisite production of costumes, props, and sets, but also put a lot of effort into the selection of actors. In addition to the two stars mentioned above, the supporting actors include the experienced Lionel Barrymore, the romantic young man Franchot Tone, Melvyn Douglas, and James Stewart. When the film was publicly screened in the United States, newspapers unanimously praised it as a great work that could compete with "叛艦喋血記" (Mutiny on the Bounty) and "舊金山" (San Francisco).

Minxin News 221

Because the character played by Liang Saizhu needs a lot of small props, such as watches, bracelets, earrings, and rings, Xiong Chun, who is in charge of managing costumes and props during filming, draws the patterns one by one in order to prevent mistakes.

In addition to serving as the photographer for "靈肉之門" (Gate of Flesh and Spirit), photographer Zhuang Guojun also serves as the photographer for "新人道" (New Humanity) with Shi Shipan, so he works in the studio almost every day.

One of the main sets of "靈肉之門" (Gate of Flesh and Spirit) - the courtroom, has been filmed a few days ago. The courtroom scene is the final closing scene of the whole play, so not only all the protagonists and main characters of the whole film appear, but also more than 50 extras and extras also participate in the filming at the same time. Before filming, director Zhong Shigen visited lawyer Wu Chengyu to refer to all the details in the courtroom.

Bu Wancang, the director of "新人道" (New Humanity), and technician Li Geng went to Qingjiangpu a few days ago to see the location of the film, and now they have returned to Shanghai.

Jin Qingyu's new work "鬩墻記" (Fratricide) has now been mostly written. "靈肉之門" (Gate of Flesh and Spirit) and "新人道" (New Humanity) will be published in one volume.

Li Minghui and the Spotted Leopard 222

Foreign women are currently in vogue for raising spotted leopards. They buy leopard cubs and use milk to raise them. When they grow up, they are tamed like cats, but they are more beautiful than cats.

However, their original animal nature has not been extinguished. If they return to the mountains and forests and hear the howling of their kind, they will suddenly feel that they belong to the mountains and forests, to their kind. Then, they will immediately hate their owners and would rather return to the mountains and forests to live a wild life of struggle and foraging. But this is free and liberated. No matter how rich and delicious the food their owners provide, it is still bound and unfree.

As the female lead Li Minghui in the new film "淸明時節" (Qingming Season), which has recently completed filming, the playwright Yao Xinong's metaphor of the spotted leopard to portray her character as the maid Chunlan is very appropriate. In the era of the maid, because of the oppression of the environment and power, she was as docile as a lamb, living a slave life. But once she came into contact with her kind - the toiling workers - and returned to their masses, when people tried to subdue her again, she completely changed. She also has a strong sense of self-esteem, resistance, and not being oppressed.

"淸明時節" (Qingming Season) depicts human self-esteem very thoroughly, and director Yang Yuqian's technique in handling the whole play is very vivid and lovely.
